üöÄ status-im/status-react - Release Notes

2.33.2 (2025-03-20)

The newest update's headline feature is adding Base support, but Status v2.33 also includes another important integration with [Mercuryo](https://mercuryo.io/) as an in-app fiat on-ramp provider. This allows Status users to buy crypto directly from Mercuryo, including subscriptions or recurring purchases.

This release also expands on the Keycard support introduced in the [previous Status v2.32 update](https://status.app/blog/status-v2-32-launched-for-mobile-and-desktop), adding more Keycard-related functionality to Status Mobile.

# Full list of changes
## Features 

- Integrated Base chain
   - ([Pull Request #21876](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21876)). The user will be able to send, bridge, SWAP, and use DApps on Base, which is one of the most active Ethereum L2.
- Added Mercuryo on-ramp provider
  - ([Pull Request #21923](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21923)). The user will be able to buy crypto with Mercuryo on-ramp provider, including recurring crypto purchases
- Easy selection for Normal, Fast, Urgent fee. The user can quickly define how fast they want their transaction to go through by selecting the Normal, Fast, or Urgent fee option.
- Added price for the receiving token in SWAPs. The user will be able to see the approximate price for the receiving token when executing a SWAP.
- Added Swap and Buy crypto features to Wallet Portfolio view. The user will be able to start Buy or Swap from the Portfolio page
- Integrating Keycard
  - Keycard factory reset (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21914). The Keycard user will be able reset their Keycard via Status Mobile
  - Seed phrase can be imported into a new Keycard (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21947). The Keycard user will be asked for an empty Keycard and a recovery phrase. The key pair associated with the recovery phrase will be put on Keycard and they will be able to set up and use Status App with their Keycard.
  - Backup keycard can be created for same seed phrase (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21990). The Keycard user will be able to create a copy of Keycard with the same PIN via Mobile.
  - Keycard PIN can be changed (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/22008). The Keycard user will be able to change the PIN of their Keycard
  - Keycard unlocking (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/22030). The Keycard user will be able to unlock their Keycard with with the recovery phrase
  - Dapp interactions can be signed with keycard (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21785). The user will be able to interact with dApps through their Keycard.
  - Add Account on Keycard (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21753). The Keycard user will be able add another account to their Keycard.
 

## Improvements

- Keycard
  - Keycard signup UI improved (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21938)
  - Recovery phrase can be seen again during profile creation (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/22009)
  - Backup flow added to the Keycard migration flow and Keycard create user flow. That flow allows user to check that backup phrase was securely stored and can be recovered (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21893)
  - Added information about what is Keycard during onboarding (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21997)
  - Recovery phrase can be seen after canceling ‚ÄúConfirm Backup‚Äù drawer (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/22108)
- Skipped unnecessary account selection when user with one account starts Send from by scanning QR (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21899)
- Activity tab opens after collectible sent (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21909)
- User gets into the app immediately after sync and approving biometrics #21884 #21890
- Assets sorted by fiat balance and collectibles sorted by name (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21908)
- Added suggestion to update profile after the onboarding (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21862)
- EIP-3770 address format removed for simplicity (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21995)
- Show communities statistics on ‚ÄúDiscover communities‚Äù page (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/22143)
- Send summary screen improved for readability (https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/22067)

## Known issues
- users may experience this "java.lang.illegalArgumentException: 16 > 0" error when signing ERC-20 bridge transaction with keycard #21936. The team is actively working on a fix for upcoming releases.

2.32.0 (2025-01-07)

#### Key Features:
- **Keycard Integration:**
  - Added the ability to sign Send, Bridge, and SWAP transactions with a Keycard, allowing users to confirm these transactions securely.
  - Introduced Keycard onboarding user flows:
    - **Create a new profile with an empty Keycard:** Enables users to set up the Status App with their empty Keycard.
    - **Login with Keycard:** Allows users to set up their Status App using their Keycard and Status key pair.
    - **Setup Keycard in App Settings:** Enables users to migrate the current profile key pair of their Status App to an empty Keycard, allowing them to use the Keycard to unlock their profile and sign transactions in the wallet.
- **Revamped and Simplified Onboarding Flows:**
  - Improved the ‚ÄúStart fresh‚Äù onboarding flow so users can set up a new Status App more quickly.
  - Enhanced the ‚ÄúUse a recovery phrase‚Äù onboarding flow so new users can set up a Status App with their Ethereum recovery phrase more efficiently.
  - Improved the ‚ÄúLog in with recovery phrase‚Äù onboarding flow so existing users can restore their Status profile using their recovery phrase faster.
  - Enhanced the ‚ÄúLog in by syncing‚Äù onboarding flow so users with an existing Status profile on another device can sync it with the Status mobile app more quickly.
- **Transaction History:**
  - Added transaction history, enabling users to view the history of transactions generated via Status.

#### Bugfixes and improvements:
- Fixed an issue with biometric login being disabled for multiple profiles due to unknown reasons, requiring the user to use a password to log in. Now, the users with  multiple status profiles won‚Äôt get their biometrics set-up turned off by Status due to unknown reasons.
- Improved the handling of offline states in Status, providing the user with more accurate and relevant data when the app is offline.
- Fixed an issue where the app could be killed or crash while in the background with push notifications enabled.
- Fixed a bug where the chat list was shared between different users.
- Fixed a problem where an empty account was randomly created.
- Improved performance for fetching the chat list for users who upgraded from v1 to v2.
- Fixed an issue where the app incorrectly displayed the setup screen despite being already set up.
- Resolved a delay in message history loading, which previously took up to 20 seconds.
- Fixed an issue where users could not tap on chats or channels after opening a profile link from a chat or viewing group details.
- Resolved a bug where the required popup did not display on a device syncing with another device multiple times using the seed phrase fallback.
- Fixed an issue where communities were being spectated even if the user had never opened them.
- Resolved incorrect drawer behavior for non-members in community chats.
- Fixed a bug where the group chat name was missing in the confirmation dialog for clearing history.
- Resolved an issue where the contact list reloaded when selecting or unselecting contacts on Android.
- Fixed a problem where the route was not rebuilt when decimals were changed or removed in fiat values on the send screen.

Status Mobile - 2.31.0 (2024-11-12)

## Summary

### Hero Feature

1. Users can now enjoy native token swaps for quick and efficient trades across Ethereum, Optimism, and Arbitrum networks.

### Bug Fixes

1. **Fix for decimal approvals** - Handles approval transactions with decimal issues. [#21326](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21326)
2. **Login profile display fix** - Resolves display issues for synced devices. [#21321](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21321)
3. **Fix for token-gated communities** - Resolves issues with joining options. [#21247](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21247)
4. **Delay in currency list fetching** - Fixes delay in loading currency data. [#21239](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21239)
5. **Error when sending ERC1155 collectibles** - Fixes sending errors for specific tokens. [#21209](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21209)
6. **Onboarding profile creation fix** - Resolves issues in creating profiles during onboarding. [#21170](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/21170)

Please, report issues/bugs in the `#feedback-mobile` channel on the Status community or via https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues.

Status Mobile - 2.29.0-beta (2024-06-13)

Please note that this version is a **beta** meant for *testing* purposes by core contributors. It's not meant for real use and makes no claims of security or integrity of funds or data in these builds.

Please report issues/bugs in the `#general` channel on the status community or via:

https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues

1.26.0 (alpha) (2024-01-17)

# Status Mobile - 1.26.0-alpha

##  Major improvements:‚Ä®
- Includes the new shards community feature
- New deep/universal links https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17721
- Numerous fixes including issues related to message handling, chat behavior, and composer functionality
- Various fixes on design feedback (can be found [here](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues?q=is%3Aissue+is%3Aclosed+label%3A%22E%3ADesign+Feedback+1.25%22+))
- Sync flow optimisation and fixes https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17311 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17342 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17340 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/16852 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17600 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17731 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17755
- Fixed issues related to token-gated communities https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17799 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17901
- Implemented various UI components and fixes 
- Introduced wallet-related components and features, including wallet account creation, activity tab, network preferences etc. **Note** that new Wallet screen is still in progress and hidden. Longtap on wallet navigation tab to switch to the New Wallet screen
- removed/refactored bunch of legacy code


## Known issues:‚Ä®
- Issues related to message reliability https://github.com/status-im/status-go/issues/4459 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues/18284 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues/18282 https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues/18301
- Android still has visible performance issues, that are logged here: https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues/16714. The issues have been investigated by @Parveshdhull, improvements will be included in next releases.

1.25.0 (Alpha) (2023-09-22)

# Status Mobile - 1.25.0-alpha

##  Major improvements:‚Ä®
- Mute community feature https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/15161
- Various fixes on design feedback (can be found [here](https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues?q=is%3Aissue+is%3Aclosed+label%3A%22E%3ADesign+Feedback+1.24%22))
- Fixing pulling images on the backend https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/16976 
- Improving identicons in https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/16193
- Fixing flows for adding members to non-token-gated community in https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/16917
- Get rid of 3-random name in https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17042
- Improved top bar in https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17170
- Improved sync stability in https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17226
- Improved animation in https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/16981
and added numerous components, bugfixes ...

## Known issues:‚Ä®

- traffic consumption is still high
- there are 2 crashes that are hardly reproducible, but you may see them - IOS can crash when it gets back from the background or after generating keys - which should be fixed with RN upgrade PR in https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/pull/17241  
- Android has visible performance issues, that are logged here: https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues/16714 - investigated and reported here https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues/16714#issuecomment-1776721533

1.24.0 (Alpha) (2023-07-20)

## Major improvements:‚Ä®

- Light-client protocol enabled (affected message reliability, now fetching/re-sending is way faster and more efficient)
- ‚Ä®Numerous design fixes  / UI fixes discussed at Porto
- ‚Ä®Animations‚Ä®‚Ä®

## Known issues:‚Ä®

- traffic consumption is still high (around 150MB/per hour, but it is already a huge improvement) - will be reported to keep track of it and investigate further‚Ä®
- there are 2 crashes that are hardly reproducible, but you may see them - the app may crash on generating keys (rare) or IOS can be crashed when it gets back from the background. We try to keep but on them and to get logs, but so far there is no pattern detected for reproducing it‚Ä®
- Android has visible performance issues, that are logged here: https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues/16714
- Small but visible UI issue with counter https://github.com/status-im/status-mobile/issues/16594 ‚Ä®‚Ä®
‚Ä¶and many others that are logged into our repo.‚Ä®‚Ä®
